calculateIntegrationScore(answers) {\n    const { q1, q2, q3, q4 } = answers;\n    \n    // Lower scores on q1, q2, q3 = better integration\n    // Higher score on q4 = better integration\n    const percentage >= 80 ? \'Integrated\' :\n                percentage >= 60 ? \'Progressing\' :\n                percentage >= 40 ? \'Aware\' : \'Fragmented\'\n    };\n}\n```\n\n####
